< Text>
We bought a classic car. I looked online to learn about DMV registration for older cars. Everyone said older cars are difficult to register at the DMV. The DMV does not always have someone on hand to go out to your car and verify the VIN number and the employees at the DMV often do not know how to correctly register your older vehicle (plus the lines are extremely long). I watched a video where a classic car collector swore he would never again not use a mobile vehicle VIN registration service. I had never heard of such a service. I did several searches looking for nearby registration services and reviews. I came upon Elite Mobile Vehicle Vin Verification & Registration. The 50 5-star reviews stood above all the others. The reviews said Joy was awesome so I gave her a call. She sounded nice on the phone and was able to come out the next day. Joy arrived on time and got right to business. She looked at the car and recorded the VIN number, then began to fill out paperwork. She has a great personality, is very professional, and has great communication skills. It took about a half hour. She took the correct paperwork to bring to the DMV and left me a temporary registration. About a week later, I received the license plates in the mail and the new registration papers. A couple of weeks later, we received the car title in the mail. Unless you enjoy dealing with the mayhem at the DMV, give Joy a call. It was well worth it.</Text>

< Review>
There's a way to tell if an auto shop is honest. Visit the dealer and take their list of services they say are necessary along with their pricing and tell the mechanic what the dealer said. If they agree with the dealer, you have a dishonest mechanic or the rare experience of a dealership not pushing unnecessary services. < text>
My daughter was saying she wanted Pho and that she and her friends went to a place on Ocean.  I found this place on google maps, but when we go here, she said this wasn't the place she went with her friends.  It was already pretty late so we got a table, at first it was less than half full.  They bring tea right away.  We ordered our food, my daughter got Pho, but I got the duck and bamboo noodle soup.  She said the Pho was ok and it smelled really good (actually when you walk in you smell the Pho broth).  The bamboo in my soup isn't your typical slice you get out of a can that many Chinese restaurants server.  I think they needed to cook the bamboo a little more, some was very chewy.  They serve a vinegar ginger sauce for the duck (they serve the duck with bones so watch out).  I wish the broth was a bit richer.

Overall the place is solid, service isn't too great, you order, you get your food, then you flag them down for the check.  My daughter never got her glass of water she request and she gave up and just drank tea instead.

About 8:30pm the place filled up quickly.  When we walked to our car, there was many people double parking, waiting for spaces.

I'll be back to try their other dish, but I'll increase my star points then.<//text>

< Review>
We hit a deer on the way up to Big Bear on our 2014 Victory Cross Country Tour at 55 mph without going down, still being able to ride it back to Palmdale and had about $8500.00 worth of damage to it. I called Tom, who is the owner of Palmdale Supercycles, and asked if I could trust him and his shop in taking good care of us and our bike because of a couple negative reviews. He reassured me that he would take good care of us and that those negative reviews were unfounded which I took his word for. We had our bike towed there and they got to work on it right away. Richard in parts was very helpful in keeping me and my girlfriend informed, he dealt professionally with our Farmers Insurance agent. The guys in service let me go back and check on the bike without being bothered by my recurring presence. We had the bike back together and in our garage in a month flat! That's with some of the parts being sent to Little Design's, which Tom had referred us to, for custom paint which the bike had before the accident. They took good care of my girlfriend and I and were very honest and informative during the whole experience. They still take good care of us to this day. I recommend Palmdale Supercycles to anyone in need of good service, parts or a new or used bike. Thank you Tom, Richard and you Pro's in service!  Ryan & Christa</Review>

<review>Simply avoid this place - far better options out there for self-wash. Here's what just happened today:

Today, my wife took our friendly, 7-year old Samoyed to Tidy Tails to leverage the self-wash station - over the years, we've grown accustomed to doing our own grooming because we found that groomers tended to leave her hair matted and unkempt causing much bigger issues. We were excited to find a reputable place via Google in Tidy Tails.

Here's the top 3 issues we encountered during the visit:

1. They don't seem to have a flat fee for self-wash! They basically assess a cost for self-wash once they see the type of breed you have. It was never clear how much this service actually costed and it seemed like a decision was made on the spot to assess a fee based on our breed - mind you, we do have a fluffy samoyed. :)

2. After the wash, my wife moved to the blow dryer station and they don't have any kind of tables to position your pet so you can actually dry efficiently. Instead, she had to sit on the floor with the dog to blow dry her.

3. ***Most important*** The owner or manager of this facility approached my wife and let her know that she would not be able to fully blow dry our dog because she didn't want her hair blowing around the store. That to me is unacceptable and defeats the purpose of offering a self-wash option to customers. What's the point in washing a dog if you can't blow dry along with it? To me, this signals laziness because the owner doesn't want to have to actually work to keep the shop clean.

My advice to those of you considering this as a grooming/self-wash option: Just go elsewhere. The lack of drying tables is a big enough pain point, but to have the lazy owner/manager amble over to let us know we will not be able to fully dry our dog despite paying the  fee they assessed us is just confusing and in my opinion, kind of useless. I know we'll be happy to spend our money elsewhere where we can have a better experience.

I'd invite the manager to reply, but they're probably out telling others to stop blow drying to care about these reviews. Seems like a failing operation to me.<//review>< name>
Jason< /name>

<Text>This place is by far the best groomers in town.

They care for sure.
